
================
# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

# Toggle a todo item by its index #
let toggle: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

# Toggle a todo item by its index #
let toggle: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
    fun

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

# Toggle a todo item by its index #
let toggle: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
    fun idx, todos ->

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

# Toggle a todo item by its index #
let toggle: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
    fun idx, todos ->
        case

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

# Toggle a todo item by its index #
let toggle: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
    fun idx, todos ->
        case todos

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

# Toggle a todo item by its index #
let toggle: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
    fun idx, todos ->
        case todos
        |

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

# Toggle a todo item by its index #
let toggle: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
    fun idx, todos ->
        case todos
        | [] => []

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

# Toggle a todo item by its index #
let toggle: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
    fun idx, todos ->
        case todos
        | [] => []

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

# Toggle a todo item by its index #
let toggle: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
    fun idx, todos ->
        case todos
        | [] => []
        | hd

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

# Toggle a todo item by its index #
let toggle: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
    fun idx, todos ->
        case todos
        | [] => []
        | hd::tl

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

# Toggle a todo item by its index #
let toggle: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
    fun idx, todos ->
        case todos
        | [] => []
        | hd::tl => if

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

# Toggle a todo item by its index #
let toggle: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
    fun idx, todos ->
        case todos
        | [] => []
        | hd::tl => if idx ==

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

        | [] => []
        | hd::tl => if idx == 0 then (

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

let toggle: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
    fun idx, todos ->

        | [] => []
        | hd::tl => if idx == 0 then (hd

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

# Toggle a todo item by its index #
let toggle: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
    fun idx, todos ->
        case todos
        | [] => []
        | hd::tl => if idx == 0 then (hd

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

let toggle: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
    fun idx, todos ->
        case todos
        | [] => []
        | hd::tl => if idx == 0 then (hd

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

# Toggle a todo item by its index #
let toggle: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
    fun idx, todos ->
        case todos
        | [] => []
        | hd::tl => if idx == 0 then (hd

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

# Toggle a todo item by its index #
let toggle: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
    fun idx, todos ->
        case todos
        | [] => []
        | hd::tl => if idx == 0 then (hd

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

# Toggle a todo item by its index #
let toggle: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
    fun idx, todos ->
        case todos
        | [] => []
        | hd::tl => if idx == 0 then (hd

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

        | [] => []
        | hd::tl => if idx == 0 then (hd

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

# Toggle a todo item by its index #
let toggle: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
    fun idx, todos ->
        case todos
        | [] => []
        | hd::tl => if idx == 0 then (hd

type Todo = (String, Bool) in

  + RemoveTodo(Int)

in

  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2

    | _ => false end

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

# Toggle a todo item by its index #
let toggle: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
    fun idx, todos ->
        case todos
        | [] => []
        | hd::tl => if idx == 0 then (hd

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

# Toggle a todo item by its index #
let toggle: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
    fun idx, todos ->
        case todos
        | [] => []
        | hd::tl => if idx == 0 then (hd

type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

# Toggle a todo item by its index #
let toggle: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
    fun idx, todos ->
        case todos
        | [] => []
        | hd::tl => if idx == 0 then (hd

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let Model.get_buffer: Model -> String =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
in

let Model.get_todo_list: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun buffer, todo_list -> todo_list
in

# Toggle a todo item by its index #
let toggle: (Int, [Todo]) -> [Todo]=
    fun idx, todos ->
        case todos
        | [] => []
        | hd::tl => if idx == 0 then (hd

type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #

  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
  + UpdateBuffer(String)
in

let Bool.eq: (Bool, Bool) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, b2) -> if b1 then b2 else !b2
in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
    d1 $== d2 && Bool.eq(s1, s2)
in

let todo_list_eq: ([Todo], [Todo]) -> Bool =
    fun xs, ys ->
    case xs, ys
    | [], [] => true
    | x::xs, y::ys => Todo.eq(x, y) && todo_list_eq(xs, ys)
    | _ => false end
in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
    b1 $== b2 && todo_list_eq(ts1, ts2)
in

  fun buffer, todo_list -> buffer
